<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Interim
Management Report</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1. Business
Activity</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON (&#147;the AIXTRON Group&#148;
or &#147;the Company&#148;) is a leading provider of deposition equipment to the
semiconductor industry. The Company&#146;s technology solutions are used by a
diverse range of customers worldwide to build advanced components for
electronic and opto-electronic applications based on compound, silicon, or
organic semiconductor materials. Such components are used in displays, signaling,
lighting, fiber optic communication systems, wireless and mobile telephony
applications, optical and electronic storage devices, computing, as well as a
range of other leading-edge technologies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company markets and
sells its products worldwide, principally through its direct sales organization
and appointed dealers and sales representatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s business
activities include developing, producing and installing equipment for coating
semiconductor materials, process engineering, consulting and training,
including ongoing customer support.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON supplies to
customers both full production-scale chemical vapor deposition systems and
small scale systems for Research and Development use and small-scale production
use.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s product range
includes customized production and research scale compound semiconductor
systems capable of depositing material films on up to 95 x two-inch diameter
wafers per single production run, or smaller multiples of 4 to 6 inch diameter
wafers, employing Metal-Organic Chemical Vapor Deposition (&#147;MOCVD&#148;) or organic
thin film deposition on up to Gen. 3.5 substrates, including Polymer Vapor
Phase Deposition (&#147;PVPD&#148;) or Organic Vapor Phase Deposition (&#147;OVPD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#148;) for Organic Light Emitting Diodes (&#147;OLED&#148;) applications or Plasma
Enhanced Chemical Vapor Phase Deposition (&#147;PECVD&#148;) for depositing complex
Carbon Nanostructures (Carbon Nanotubes or Nanowires). AIXTRON also
manufactures full production and research scale deposition systems for silicon
semiconductor market applications capable of depositing material films on
wafers of up to 300 mm diameter, employing technologies such as: Chemical Vapor
Deposition (&#147;CVD&#148;), Atomic Vapor Deposition (&#147;AVD<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#148;)
and Atomic Layer Deposition (&#147;ALD&#148;).</p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\105533\09-12641-1\task3540282\12641-1-be-01.htm',USER='105533',CD='May  7 13:55 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2.
Important Factors of the Reporting Period</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Gross
margin increased despite revenue drop</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reflecting the global recession and the
currently difficult market environment, first quarter revenues of EUR 46.2m
were 26% lower year on year and 44% below the Q4/2008 level.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Nevertheless, the gross margin increased by 2
percentage points to 45% compared to Q4/2008 and, as such, was 6 percentage
points higher in comparison to Q1/2008.&#160; This
improvement was principally due to a stronger US-Dollar rate, a more favorable
revenue mix and a flexible production model employed by the Company.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>As previously predicted, at EUR 31.2m the
equipment order intake in Q1 was less than Q4/2008 (-23%) and also 64% down
year on year.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 16.0pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Positive
contribution of other operating income</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>With contributions to other operating income
from capital gains on the disposal of the office building in Aachen and a
compensation payment for a cancelled order, EBIT came in at EUR 7.6m (16%
margin) in Q1/2009.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Without the above mentioned effects, EBIT
would have been EUR 3.8m, which would have translated into an EBIT margin of
8%, slightly below Q4/2008. In the current market environment, even this
residual margin level is encouraging and further evidence of the flexible and
cost-effective organization built up within the group.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Cash and Cash Equivalents incl. cash deposits
(March&nbsp;31, 2009: EUR 81.6m; December&nbsp;31, 2008: EUR 70.5m) remained
high in the quarter, being positively impacted by the cash inflow from the
office building sale of EUR 6.7m.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 47.15pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Continued
US-Dollar strength</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Q1/2009 average exchange rate against the
Euro was USD 1.30, 15% stronger than the USD 1.50 average of Q1/2008, which has
in turn positively influenced AIXTRON&#146;s Q1/2009 revenues and EBIT.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>This beneficial exchange rate movement in the
year on year period to March&nbsp;31, and the 5% improvement during Q1/2009
underlined the recent fundamental trend towards a stronger US-Dollar.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 26.4pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5',FILE='C:\JMS\105533\09-12641-1\task3540282\12641-1-be-01.htm',USER='105533',CD='May  7 13:55 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Final
Customer Acceptance of Plastic Logic System</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The final acceptance documentation for the
first Gen 3.5 large-area deposition tool, delivered, installed and commissioned
at Plastic Logic&#146;s Dresden facility during the second half of 2008, has now
been signed off by the customer at the end of Q1/2009. Consequently, the total
revenue of this previously unproven technology was recorded within Q1/2009.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The successful system acceptance provides
further evidence of AIXTRON&#146;s ability to diversify its core deposition
technology into new emerging market opportunities.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The tool is being used by Plastic Logic to
further develop and deposit the key organic dielectric layer within their
manufacturing process for flexible organic TFT backplanes for use in a highly
innovative wireless electronic paper application. Pilot trials using the
Plastic Logic Reader are planned by the customer for the second half of 2009
and commercial products are due in the market in 2010. The electronic reader
features a large, thin, lightweight and robust form factor that is about the
size of an 8.5 x 11-inch pad of paper and weighs less than many printed
magazines.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>In February&nbsp;and March, Plastic Logic
made two announcements concerning agreements made with its first subscription
content partners, including newspapers such as The Financial Times, USA TODAY,
The Detroit Free Press and the Detroit News.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 19.7pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">End
customer ordering frequency underpinning volatility in utilization rates</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b>Increased market nervousness towards the end
of last year had already lead to significant reductions in inventories
throughout the customer supply chain, which in turn lead to very low
utilization rates at our customers&#146; production facilities during Q4 and at the
beginning of Q1/2009. A characteristic of the most recent inventory
replenishment demand we have seen mid to late Q1, is that, in contrast to 12
months ago, customers throughout the supply chain are currently placing
smaller, short demand orders.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Consequently, we have seen recent evidence of
increased volatility in customers&#146; utilization rates, which is likely to remain
until customer confidence returns, which then could be evidenced by extended
purchasing commitments of greater volume.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
development could potentially be one signal of stabilization prior to a
sustainable recovery.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Currently, however, many customers continue
to claim that they are still unable to forecast demand beyond even the next
month and have consequently remained more reluctant towards making longer term
purchasing commitments.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 15.4pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='6',FILE='C:\JMS\105533\09-12641-1\task3540282\12641-1-be-01.htm',USER='105533',CD='May  7 13:55 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">New
strategic LED-ventures continue to emerge</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>In March&nbsp;2009, Samsung Electronics
announced that it will set up a new LED production company in Korea in April&nbsp;by
merging its LED businesses into an internal 50-50 joint venture between Samsung
Electro-Mechanics and Samsung Electronics.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Recently, other Asian LCD-producers have also
been making announcements of their intent to enter into the LED segment to
secure a supply of components.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>These new ventures illustrate that, despite
the gloomy overall economic environment, the increased interest and commitment
in LED technology and markets remains undiminished while new application
opportunities continue to emerge. This is consistent with AIXTRON&#146;s view that
the medium to long-term fundamentals for the LED industry remain strong.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 18.45pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">New
international thin film solar-cell project</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>During Q1/2009, the EU-funded &#147;ROD_SOL&#148;
research project was formally started by a consortium of 10 leading European
materials oriented research institutes and industrial partners, including
AIXTRON, together with the IBM T.J. Watson Research Center from the USA.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The project aims at providing novel concepts
for thin film solar cells based on nanorods (better known as nanowires),
focusing on the potential for solar cell efficiencies in excess of the current
10% limit that comes from the current structural and cell design limitations.
Moreover, it is believed that the targeted thin film concept, using thin active
semiconductor films and more cost effective substrates, such as glass or
polymeric or metal foils, will enable more competitive production costs in due
course.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>AIXTRON will bring to the project the company&#146;s
core competence in the optimization of MOCVD technology for the deposition of
Silicon-nanorods and group-III nitride nanorods as a key prerequisite for the
industrialization of such thin film solar cells.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 16.4pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">World
Record efficiency for multi-junction solar cells</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Researchers at the Fraunhofer Institute for
Solar Energy Systems ISE have recently achieved a record efficiency of 41.1%
for the conversion of sunlight into electricity.&#160; Sunlight has been concentrated by a factor of
454 and focused onto a small 5 mm&#178; multi-junction solar cell made out of
GaInP/GaInAs/Ge (gallium indium phosphide, gallium indium arsenide on a
germanium substrate).</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The world-renowned Fraunhofer ISE has been a
leading developer of such multi-junction solar cell technology since 1999. The
devices they have developed are a special type of solar cell using III-V
semiconductor compounds, produced using a MOCVD reactor from AIXTRON.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 32.1pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3. Results
of Operations</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.1.
Development of Revenues</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first three
months of 2009, AIXTRON recorded revenues of EUR 46.2m, a decrease of EUR
16.4m, or 26%, compared to EUR 62.6m in the same period last year. The positive
effects of a stronger US-Dollar rate could not entirely compensate for weaker
revenues in line with the current investment cycle and the effects of the
global recession.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The decline in revenues was
largely driven by weaker sales of compound semiconductor deposition equipment in
the quarter (Q1/2009: EUR 41.9m or 91% of total revenues; Q1/2008: EUR 47.8 m
or 76%), being purchased by customers predominantly for the production of LEDs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenues from silicon
semiconductor deposition equipment, NAND-Flash and DRAM-production systems,
decreased to EUR 0.2m (Q1/2008: EUR 8.3m or 13%). This is the result of the
continued depressed memory market conditions, being made more severe by the
global recession, and consequently suppressed capital spending by AIXTRON&#146;s
customers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total equipment sales
generated 91% of total revenues in Q1/2009 versus 89% in Q1/2008. The remaining
revenues were generated by sales of spare parts and service, where the decline
in volume is due to customers cutting back on spare orders and reducing spare
inventories in the current environment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Revenues</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.96%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">68% of total revenues in
Q1/2009 were delivered to customers in Asia. This was 15 percentage points
below the 83% recorded in Q1/2008, reflecting the inventory reduction process
particularly in Asia. The comparatively high European revenue share (25% in Q1/2009
versus 7% in Q1/2008) was significantly influenced by the Plastic Logic revenue
being recorded in Q1/2009. The remaining revenues, with a 7% share, were
generated in the USA.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cost of
sales </font></b>decreased
significantly year on year by 34% in absolute terms from EUR 38.1m in Q1/2008
to EUR 25.2m in Q1/2009, whilst cost of sales relative to revenues improved
considerably from 61% to 55%. This improved result comes from a more favorable
revenue mix (with a higher percentage of final acceptances in the quarter) and
a favorable USD/EUR exchange rate.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='9',FILE='C:\JMS\105566\09-12641-1\task3537736\12641-1-be-03.htm',USER='105566',CD='May  6 18:33 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Consequently, the 14%
reduction, year on year, in the Company&#146;s <b>gross
profit</b> to EUR 21.0m in Q1/2009 (Q1/2008: EUR 24.5m) does not reflect
the degree of reduction in revenues (-26%) and resulted in a 6 percentage-point
higher <b>gross margin</b> of 45%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compared to the first three
months of 2008, Q1/2009 <b>operating costs</b>
decreased by 15% to EUR 13.4m in absolute terms. At the same time, operating
costs relative to revenues in percentage terms increased only slightly from 25%
in Q1/2008 to 29% in Q1/2009, influenced by the following factors:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The decrease of <b>selling expenses</b> by 43% to EUR 4.6m
(Q1/2008: EUR 8.0m) was mainly due to lower volume related variable sales
commissions. Selling costs relative to revenues decreased to 10% (Q1/2008:
13%).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">General
administration expenses</font></b>
remained stable in absolute terms at EUR 4.6m in Q1/2009 (Q1/2008: EUR 4.5m).
However, with lower revenues, general and administration expenses relative to
revenues increased by 3 percentage points to 10% due to the fixed cost effect.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compared to the same period
last year, <b>Research and Development costs</b>
increased by 31% in absolute terms in Q1/2009 to EUR 8.9m, the largest element
being the expense for one publicly funded R&amp;D project (&#147;Dual Logic&#148;) of EUR
1.6m. R&amp;D costs relative to revenues increased by 8 percentage points from
11% to 19%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The continued focus on
R&amp;D (for both for Silicon and Compound equipment) is driven by our
determination to remain a major player in markets judged by many to be
significant growth opportunities for many years to come.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net <b>other operating income and expenses</b>
increased by 34% to a net income of EUR 4.7m in the first three months of 2009
(Q1/2008: EUR 3.5m).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Included in the other
operating income and expenses of Q1/2009 are hedging effects from the
USD/EUR-rate accounting for a net expense of EUR 1.4m (Q1/2008: hedging income
of net EUR 2.4m).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='10',FILE='C:\JMS\105566\09-12641-1\task3537736\12641-1-be-03.htm',USER='105566',CD='May  6 18:33 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Also included are the gain
from the sale of the Aachen office building (EUR 1.3m) and a one-time
compensation payment for a cancelled order (EUR 2.5m). Without those two items
of a total EUR 3.8m, net other operating income and expenses would have
resulted in EUR 0.9m of income.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With a 26% revenue
reduction, the <b>operating income (EBIT) </b>decreased
to a lesser extent, by 13% to EUR 7.6m or 16% margin in Q1/2009 (Q1/2008: EUR
8.7m; 14% margin), supported by the positive USD/EUR-effect, the favorable
revenue mix, and the benefit of the two above mentioned events in the quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Even excluding these
benefits to other operating income, EBIT would have been EUR 3.8m in Q1/2009.
Relative to revenues, with a margin of 8%, the &#147;residual&#148; EBIT of Q1/2009 would
have been 6 percentage points below the Q1/2008 EBIT margin and slightly lower
sequentially. So, despite the difficult global market environment, AIXTRON&#146;s
EBIT ratio remained resilient, even after taking into account the two
above-mentioned effects in Q1/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Result
before taxes </font></b>decreased
16% from EUR 9.3m in Q1/2008 to EUR 7.9m in Q1/2009.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON recorded a <b>tax expense </b>of EUR 2.4m of the profit
before tax in the first three months of 2009, with an effective tax rate of
30%. In comparison to Q1/2008 (EUR 3.4m or 36% of the profit before taxes), the
Q1/2009 tax rate was lower due to the utilization of tax losses in the quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Q1/2009 <b>net income</b> was EUR 5.5m, 7% down year on
year from EUR 5.9m in Q1/2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.3. Development of Orders</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='11',FILE='C:\JMS\105566\09-12641-1\task3537736\12641-1-be-03.htm',USER='105566',CD='May  6 18:33 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s total <b>equipment order intake</b> declined by 64%
compared to the previous years&#146; first quarter and by 23% sequentially,
reflecting the current investment cycle in the LED industry and the effects of
the global credit crisis and recession.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However, as we enter the
second quarter of the year, there is a more positive tone to discussions we are
having with customers, leading to a slightly more cautious optimism on how
Q2/2009 may develop.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Order intake for compound
semiconductor equipment, being used by customers predominantly for the
production of LED end-market applications, decreased by 60% to EUR 30.6m from
EUR 77.3m in Q1/2008, and represents 98% of the total value of equipment orders
received by AIXTRON in the first three months of 2009 (90% in Q1/2008).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The proportion of orders
received for silicon semiconductor equipment, compared to total equipment
orders received in the first three months of 2009, dropped to 2%, from 10% in
Q1/2008. In absolute numbers, the order intake for silicon semiconductor
equipment decreased by 93% to EUR 0.6m in Q1/2009 from EUR 8.2m in Q1/2008, due
to the continued deterioration of the memory market environment, consequently
characterized by extremely restrictive customer capital spending.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a result of weaker order
intake, the <b>equipment order backlog</b>
of EUR 100.7m at March&nbsp;31, 2009 is 36% lower than at the same point in
time in 2008 (EUR 157.3m). The Management expects that about EUR 96m of that
backlog will be converted into revenues by the end of the year 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The order backlog for
compound semiconductor equipment was EUR 93.5m as of March&nbsp;31, 2009 (93%
of backlog), representing a 39% decrease year on year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The remaining backlog figure
of EUR 7.2m (7% of backlog) is made up of silicon semiconductor equipment
orders convertible into revenues in 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.45pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a matter of internal
policy, AIXTRON records only equipment orders as actual order intake and order
backlog, if the Company has received a firm purchase order, an agreed deposit
and a customer-confirmed delivery date.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='12',FILE='C:\JMS\105566\09-12641-1\task3537736\12641-1-be-03.htm',USER='105566',CD='May  6 18:33 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4.
Financial Position and Net Assets</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company recorded no <b>bank borrowings</b> as of March&nbsp;31, 2009
and December&nbsp;31, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b>equity ratio</b> increased to 73% as of March&nbsp;31,
2009, from 68% as of December&nbsp;31, 2008, principally due to higher retained
earnings and lower and inventories.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The AIXTRON Group&#146;s <b>capital expenditures</b> of the first quarter
of 2009 amounted to EUR 2.9m (Q1/2008: EUR 3.6m), the large majority of which
was related to purchases of technical equipment (including testing and
laboratory equipment).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash and
cash equivalents including cash deposits</font></b> increased by 16% to EUR 81.6m (EUR 76.6m +
EUR 5.0m) as of March&nbsp;31, 2009 compared to EUR 70.5m (EUR 67.5m + EUR
3.0m) as of December&nbsp;31, 2008. Included in the period end Cash position
are cash items of EUR 6.7m arising from the sale of the Aachen office building.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>property, plant and equipment </b>decreased to
EUR 34.0m as per March&nbsp;31, 2009 (EUR 39.3m as of December&nbsp;31, 2008),
principally due to the sale of the Aachen office building. Depreciations
continue to generally offset investments in technical equipment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The increase in recorded <b>goodwill</b> from EUR 58.7m as per December&nbsp;31,
2008 to EUR 61.1m as per March&nbsp;31, 2009 resulted from currency
translation. There were no additions or impairments in the first three months
of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>other intangible assets </b>decreased from EUR
10.3m as per December&nbsp;31, 2008 to EUR 9.7m as per March&nbsp;31, 2009
principally due to depreciation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Trade
receivables</font></b> decreased
from EUR 38.8m as of December&nbsp;31, 2008 to EUR 31.5m as of March&nbsp;31,
2009 due to the reduced business volume.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.45pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">5.
Opportunities and Risks</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON believes that the
following market trends and <b>opportunities</b>
of the relevant end user markets could have a positive effect on future
business:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Short Term</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Continuing increase of capacity for the
production of LED backlighting for LCD-Screens (liquid crystal displays) and
high-performance laser products.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Further increased adoption of LEDs in
automotive (e.g. interior lighting, headlights and rear lights), street
lighting or other applications.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 35.8pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mid Term</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Further development progress leading to a
broader application of LEDs in general/interior lighting.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increased emergence of high volume Silicon
Carbide (SiC) production applications and emerging hybrid automotive and
photovoltaic transistor applications.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Development of plastic electronics / flexible
organic TFT backplanes.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Development of next generation NAND and DRAM
memory applications.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increased development activity for
specialized compound solar cell applications.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Potential government support for energy efficient
and environmentally friendly lighting applications.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 48.7pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Long Term</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Progress in research activities leading to
technologies for OLED lighting and organic material large area deposition.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Intensified activity in the development of
new complex semiconductor material applications as substituting materials in
the silicon semiconductor industry.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Development of new applications using Carbon
Nanostructures (Carbon Nanotubes or Carbon Nanowires).</p>

<p style="margin:0in 123.8pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">14</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON is exposed to a
series of <b>risks</b> which are
described in detail in chapter 7. &#147;Risk Report&#148; of the Annual Report 2008 and
in the section &#147;Risk Factors&#148; in AIXTRON&#146;s 2008 20-F-Report, which has been
filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission on March&nbsp;12, 2009.
Copies of the Company&#146;s most recent Annual Report and Form&nbsp;20-F are
available on the Company&#146;s website at http://www.aixtron.com (sections &#147;Investors/Reports&#148;
and &#147;Investors/US-Listing&#148;), as well as on the SEC&#146;s website at http://www.sec.gov.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April&nbsp;7, 2009, the
court in Aachen judged in AIXTRON&#146;s favor in the German action for a negative
declaratory judgment against International Rectifier Corporation (&#147;I.R.&#148;). The
German counterclaim of I.R. was therefore dismissed. However, I.R. has the
right to appeal against this judgment until mid May&nbsp;2009. The U.S. legal
action initiated by I.R. remains ongoing, and AIXTRON AG continues to reject
all allegations involved and continues to defend itself against the allegations
and claims raised in the action.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first three
months of 2009, AIXTRON Management were not aware of any further significant
additions or changes in the risks as described in the 2008 Annual Report/20-F-Report
referred to above.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">15</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">6. Outlook</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Whilst recognizing the
impact on order intake and revenue levels of the currently difficult business
environment, the Company remains confident in its business model. AIXTRON also
continues to be optimistic about the evident medium to long-term trends towards
the increasing adoption of LED technologies in a wide range of applications and
the consequent positive effect on future order intake.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As we enter the second
quarter of the year there is a more positive tone to discussions we are having
with customers. This development persuades us that we can now offer an initial
revenue and EBIT guidance range for fiscal year 2009. (We had previously only
offered, in March&nbsp;2009, an EBIT break-even forecast at EUR 170m of
revenues in 2009.)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We believe that in fiscal
year 2009, AIXTRON can deliver revenues in the range of EUR 200 &#150; 220m and an
EBIT margin in the range of 10 &#150; 11%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Management will continue
to review this position on a regular basis and will advise the market if there
are any further developments that warrant a further update.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.45pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the next nine months
of the year, the Company plans to continue to invest in laboratory equipment
and to complete the implementation of the group-wide SAP Enterprise Software
System.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company continues to
have sufficient funds to be able to support the planned business activities in
the foreseeable future.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As at March&nbsp;31, 2009,
AIXTRON had no binding agreements for participation financing, company
acquisition or transfers of parts of the Company.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">16</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Additional
Disclosures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1.
Accounting Policies</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This consolidated interim
financial report of AIXTRON AG has been prepared in accordance with
International Financial Reporting Standards (IFRS) applicable for Interim
Financial Reporting, IAS 34.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The accounting policies
adopted in this interim financial report are consistent with those followed in
the preparation of the Group&#146;s annual financial statements for the year ended December&nbsp;31,
2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The consolidated interim
financial statements of AIXTRON AG include the following operating subsidiaries
(collectively referred to as &#147;AIXTRON&#148;, &#147;the AIXTRON Group&#148;, or &#147;the Company&#148;):
AIXTRON,&nbsp;Inc., Sunnyvale, California (USA); AIXTRON Ltd., Cambridge
(United Kingdom); AIXTRON AB, Lund (Sweden); AIXTRON Korea Co. Ltd., Seoul
(South Korea); AIXTRON KK, Tokyo (Japan); and AIXTRON Taiwan Co. Ltd.,
Hsinchu-City (Taiwan). There were no significant changes in the consolidated
group of companies in comparison with December&nbsp;31, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.35pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">21</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2. Segment
Reporting</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following segment
information has been prepared in accordance with IFRS 8 &#147;Operating Segments&#148;.
AIXTRON has only one business segment for reporting purposes, the information
provided relates only to geographical areas.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 14.3pt .0001pt 0in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company markets and
sells its products in Asia, Europe, and the United States, mainly through its
direct sales organization and cooperation partners.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In presenting information on
the basis of geographical areas, revenue is based on the location of customers.
Assets are based on the geographical location of the assets.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As part of the Genus Inc.
acquisition transaction, which was completed in March&nbsp;2005, a trust for
the employee stock options of the Genus employees was set up, into which an
appropriate number of AIXTRON ADSs were deposited.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4.
